*v110 - Session 102 CLOSE — **Group H Cycle H5 + Follow-up SHIPPED end-to-end. BrainWise HTML Authoring Spec produced as standalone deliverable. H6 v1 scope fully locked.** All three deliverables verified by Cole's smoke test on `ptp_test_article.html` (Group H canonical reference, 522 lines): eyebrow + deck + lede + byline + numbered section rules (01-04) + pullquote + callout + domain grid with 5 rows + index row with TRI/RSI cards + footer-meta tag strip all imported as correctly-styled BrainWise nodes. Smoke test PASSED. **H5 Cycle 1 (atom simples) SHIPPED — 20 files modified, 2 skipped.** Modified: Audio, AuthorBio, Chart, CodeDiff, CTA, Callout, Embed, FooterMeta, Footnotes, FurtherReading, ImageCompare, Math, Poll, Pullquote, RelatedArticles, StatCallout, SubscribeBlock, Terminal, Definition mark, FootnoteRef mark. Skipped (Lovable pushback accepted as architecturally correct): ImageGallery, StatGrid — wrapper-only fallback rules would fail ProseMirror content-expression coercion (`newsletterImage+`, `newsletterStatCallout+`) silently because the wrappers expect specific child node types and external markup doesn't produce them; children reparent naturally to the parent block flow without the wrapper, which is acceptable behavior. Image.ts excluded from H5 entirely — image import flow is handled upstream by `rewriteImgsToSyntheticFigures` in ImportHtmlModal.tsx (Session 101 H4 architecture). Embed deviation: `twitter` and `loom` map to `provider: "generic"` since EmbedProvider TypeScript union is `"youtube" | "spotify" | "vimeo" | "generic"` and was not extended. The `blockquote.twitter-tweet` rule was dropped from spec since it would require provider union extension. FootnoteRef cross-element lookup (Path 1) shipped: `sup > a[href^="#fn-N"]` rule walks `el.ownerDocument.getElementById(id)` to read the footnote body content from a separate footnotes block — first H5 example of cross-element parseHTML semantics. **H5 Cycle 2 (composites) SHIPPED — 3 files modified, 7 skipped with §151 doc-comment markers.** Shipped: Checklist (parent + ChecklistItem child), Citations (parent + CitationEntry child), Disclosure (parent + DisclosureSummary child). Skipped (schema-blocked, documented in source with §151 markers): DomainGrid, FourColumn, IndexRow, KeyMoments, StepList, ThreeColumn, TwoColumn. Two/Three/FourColumn parents have EXACT-count content expressions (no `+`) making them genuinely impossible to satisfy from external markup via parseHTML alone — `newsletterTwoColumnPane newsletterTwoColumnPane` (no plus quantifier) requires precisely two panes, no more no less, and external markup can't be coerced into that shape without preprocessing. StepList has a two-layer fail: parent strict content expression PLUS Step requires `heading block*` which means first child must be a heading; external step content rarely leads with a heading. **H5 Follow-up cycle 3 SHIPPED — 5 files, includes 2 REVERSALS of Cycle 2 skip decisions.** After Cole's smoke test exposed gaps on the canonical test article: (1) Pullquote.ts added `div.pullquote`, `div[class~="pullquote"]` matches (Cycle 1 missed these); (2) FooterMeta.ts added `div.footer-meta`, `footer.footer-meta`, `div[class~="footer-meta"]` matches (Cycle 1 missed these); (3) SectionRule.ts `div.section-rule` getAttrs now reads visible `.section-rule-num` and `.section-rule-title` children when canonical `data-*` attrs are absent, and auto-promotes `style` attr to `"numbered"` when a visible number marker is present (preserves "01" / "02" / "03" / "04" markers from the test article); (4) **DomainGrid.ts REVERSED from Cycle 2 skip** — added parent (`div.domain-grid`, `section.domain-grid`) and child (`div.domain-row`) fallback rules with TEXT_NODE-filtered label and count_value parsing from rendered DOM text; paired-rule pattern satisfies the `newsletterDomainRow+` strict content expression because both parent AND child fallbacks fire together; (5) **IndexRow.ts REVERSED from Cycle 2 skip** — added parent (`div.index-row`) and child (`div.index-card`) fallback rules with `.tri → navy` and `.rsi → orange` accent_color inference from CSS class names. **§151 amendment locked Session 102: "wrapper-strict-child" class of composite nodes is NOT universally unfixable.** Paired-rule patterns (both parent + child class fallbacks shipped together at priority 51) DO satisfy strict content expressions of the form `newsletterChildType+`, because ProseMirror runs both rules together during parse and the child matches feed the parent's content expression. The genuinely-unfixable cases are narrower than Cycle 2 assumed: only (a) exact-count content expressions without `+` quantifier (`A A`, `A A A`, `A A A A`) and (b) heading-first content expressions (Step's `heading block*` requirement). The Cycle 2 skip set should be re-examined for any node whose parent expression uses `child+`; paired-rule pattern likely applies. Remaining genuinely-blocked nodes: TwoColumn, ThreeColumn, FourColumn (exact-count), StepList (heading-first). KeyMoments may be re-evaluable. **BrainWise HTML Authoring Spec produced as standalone deliverable** at `/mnt/user-data/outputs/BRAINWISE_HTML_AUTHORING_SPEC.md` (796 lines). Complete authoring contract for LLMs producing BrainWise-importable HTML: 24 supported import patterns documented with class names and example markup, all 12 inline marks covered, 13 import-friendly block patterns with class names and internal selectors detailed, documented limitations for 7 schema-blocked composites, anti-patterns section, optional CSS template for preview rendering, pre-output checklist. Verified against shipped state of all 37 nodes + 10 marks via direct source inspection. Key authoring constraints documented: H1 must be dropped from body content (StarterKit configured with `levels: [2, 3, 4]` only, H1 is article title field), URLs must pass `isSafeHttpUrl()` validation (no `javascript:`, `data:`, etc.). SSRF defense includes IPv4 private ranges + 127.x + 169.254.x + 172.16-31.x + 192.168.x + 0.x + cloud metadata; IPv6 ::1, ::, fc00::/7, fe80::/10, IPv4-mapped (`::ffff:a.b.c.d`); `.local` mDNS blocked; manual-redirect fetch with per-hop URL re-validation (max 5 hops); schemes restricted to http/https. Limits: 30 images/request, 10MB per image (Content-Length pre-check + streamed byte cap), 8s per-image timeout via AbortController, 120s aggregate phase deadline (under Supabase 150s wall clock), worker-pool concurrency=5. Cole's reconciliation pushback that "apikey may be enforced at gateway layer before function code runs" was empirically confirmed and is the correct gateway-vs-function diagnostic frame for future curl-test interpretation. **H4 frontend refactor SHIPPED via Lovable single cycle.** Commit `5288c63` "Refactored client-side HTML import" — 651 → 846 LOC on `src/components/newsletter/editor/ImportHtmlModal.tsx`, +195 LOC delta. Synthetic-figure helper handles three cases: skip-if-already-wrapped (round-trip case), enclosing-figure replacement (Substack/Medium pattern), bare-img replacement. This is the H5 gap — NOT an H4 regression. Root cause is upstream and structural: most H2 parseHTML rules across Sessions 96-100 were written for round-trip optimization (newsletter authors save + reload their own content, which always carries `data-newsletter-*` sentinels from renderHTML) but were never extended with class-based or tag-based fallback selectors for external content ingestion. **H5 pre-audit completed in-session via Python script** (`/home/claude/h4/audit_parsehtml.py`) reading every node + mark file's `parseHTML()` block, classifying each selector as round-trip-only (data-attr or BW-namespaced class) or import-friendly (generic class/tag external sources emit). No stored IDs, no sync, no orphans by construction. **CSS counter alignment achieved via two-counter mechanism**: inline refs use custom `footnote-counter` (counter-reset on `.newsletter-prose`, counter-increment on `[data-newsletter-footnote-ref]`, displayed via `::after` pseudo-element with `counter(footnote-counter)`). Footnotes block uses native `<ol>` list-style decimal. Both walk document order so numbers align by construction regardless of Footnotes block placement (top, middle, or end of article). Cron job `prune_newsletter_subscribe_attempts_daily` at `15 6 * * *` ships active, runs as postgres role per `cron.schedule()` default (Lovable v2 pattern from Session 93 — the explicit `cron.schedule_in_database(..., username := 'postgres')` form requires superuser the MCP role lacks; using `cron.schedule()` produces identical job registration with username='postgres' assigned automatically by Supabase). Per §131 cron slot collision audit ran pre-migration: 6:15 confirmed free. Smoke test: `SELECT public.prune_newsletter_subscribe_attempts()` returned `{success:true, deleted_count:0, cutoff:<now-24h>, pruned_at:<now>}` against empty production table. Permissions: REVOKE EXECUTE FROM PUBLIC, anon, authenticated — cron runs as postgres superuser regardless. (2) **G2.2 SHIPPED — `session94_newsletter_pending_confirmation_expiry_function_and_cron` + `session94_newsletter_pending_confirmation_expiry_rewrite_to_delete`.** First migration created `expire_pending_newsletter_confirmations()` SECDEF function flipping `newsletter_subscribers` rows with status='pending_confirmation' AND created_at < now() - 7d to status='unsubscribed' + setting unsubscribed_at. Cron job at `25 6 * * *` ships active. **Q14 design correction surfaced before G2.3 draft:** flipping abandoned-pending rows to 'unsubscribed' creates an ambiguity with user-initiated unsubscribes since Q7.C policy locks unsubscribed addresses out of re-subscription. Path A locked: rewrite function body to DELETE the abandoned-pending row entirely (frees email for fresh subscribe; audit trail preserved in newsletter_subscribe_attempts and email_logs which the cron does NOT touch). Rewrite migration applied immediately; verified body contains DELETE not UPDATE; returns `{success:true, deleted_count:N, cutoff:<now-7d>, expired_at:<now>}`. The newsletter_subscribers table represents *current* subscription state; abandoned drafts are not current state. (3) **G2.3 SHIPPED — `session94_newsletter_subscribe_RPCs` + `session94_newsletter_rpcs_revoke_public`.** Five RPCs in one migration: `_send_newsletter_confirmation_email_internal(uuid, text)` private helper (defined first so subscribe_to_newsletter can PERFORM it; locked from anon/authenticated/PUBLIC); `subscribe_to_newsletter(text, text, text)` anon-callable with Q13.A anti-enumeration (always returns generic success); `confirm_newsletter_subscription(text)` anon-callable with Q15 distinct success/failure responses (legitimate to surface invalid_or_expired_token to the user who clicked the link); `unsubscribe_from_newsletter(text)` anon-callable idempotent; `list_newsletter_subscribers(text, integer, integer)` super_admin only with §111 wrapper-shape return + assert_super_admin() gate. Locked Q-decisions in migration body: Q7.A (existing pending → rotate confirmation token + re-send), Q7.B (existing confirmed → silent no-op), Q7.C (existing unsubscribed/bounced/complained → silent no-op preserving Resend reputation), Q8 (5/hr/IP rolling rate limit), Q9 Variant 2 (warmer/branded copy: subject "One click to confirm — BrainWise newsletter" + CTA "Yes, send me the newsletter"), Q11.A (Turnstile verification via pg_net polling Cloudflare siteverify inside the RPC — 30-iteration 100ms-sleep loop polls net._http_response, total 3s max wait, fail-closed on timeout), Q12.A (synchronous email dispatch via send-email Edge Function), Q16 (32-byte gen_random_bytes → base64url → SHA-256 hex hash pattern, raw token in URL only, hash persists), Q17 (apex `brainwiseenterprises.com` for confirmation + unsubscribe URLs), Q19 (unsubscribe link in confirmation email footer for CAN-SPAM/GDPR transactional compliance), Q20.α (refined: generate unsubscribe token once on first send if absent; on re-send rotate the unsubscribe token — accepts that prior unopened email's unsub link breaks since they haven't acted on it anyway). Pgcrypto search_path on all four token-handling RPCs includes `extensions` per §129. Anti-enumeration in subscribe_to_newsletter: email format validation failure → generic success; turnstile token absent or invalid → generic success; rate-limited IP → generic success; existing confirmed/unsubscribed/bounced/complained → generic success (no email sent, no DB change). Only no-row case generates fresh confirmation token + INSERT + sends email; existing pending_confirmation rotates token + UPDATE + re-sends email. Frontend cannot distinguish branches. Post-apply, follow-up migration `session94_newsletter_rpcs_revoke_public` REVOKEd default PUBLIC grants Postgres auto-creates on new functions (the original migration had GRANT TO anon + authenticated explicitly but did not REVOKE FROM PUBLIC; tightening for §82 explicit-grant discipline + defense-in-depth on list_newsletter_subscribers which now has authenticated-only explicit grant on top of internal assert_super_admin gate). All five RPCs SECDEF, all return jsonb, all search_path locked. Smoke tests: confirm with invalid token returned `{success:false, error:'invalid_or_expired_token'}`; unsubscribe with invalid token returned `{success:false, error:'invalid_unsubscribe_token'}`; subscribe with malformed email returned `{success:true, message:'Check your email for a confirmation link.'}` (anti-enumeration working); subscribe with valid email + dummy Turnstile token returned generic success + verified via net._http_response that Cloudflare siteverify was called and rejected the dummy token (full chain verified end-to-end: Vault read of CLOUDFLARE_TURNSTILE_SECRET → pg_net.http_post → Cloudflare response polled → branch decision); list_newsletter_subscribers as super_admin (impersonating via set_config('request.jwt.claims', ...)) returned `{items:[], total_count:0, limit:10, offset:0, status_filter:null}` wrapper shape; same RPC as anon raised `42501: Permission denied: caller is not a BrainWise super admin` from assert_super_admin(). Production tables remain empty post-smoke-test. (4) **G2.4a SHIPPED — `session94_newsletter_resend_audience_sync` + `sync-resend-audience` Edge Function v1.** Edge Function deployed first (Class B per §107, verify_jwt:false, INTERNAL_FUNCTION_SECRET gate with constant-time safeEqual). Implements Resend's Nov-2025 contacts overhaul: contacts are now global to the Resend account (no audience_id required for POST/PATCH/DELETE per discovery during recon). `action='add'` → POST `/contacts` `{email, unsubscribed:false}` (idempotent — Resend re-creates or returns existing contact_id); `action='remove'` → PATCH `/contacts/<email>` `{unsubscribed:true}` (Q25.A soft-unsubscribe — keeps Resend contact record for analytics, Resend skips unsubscribed contacts on broadcasts automatically). Reads `RESEND_API_KEY` from Edge Function Secrets (same key already used by send-email Edge Function — confirmed via 7-day email_logs query showing 46 successful sends across 10 email_types). Best-effort: errors logged + returned in `{synced:false}` body but never throw 5xx; caller treats this as fire-and-forget per Q27.A. On successful add, writes returned Resend contact_id back to `newsletter_subscribers.resend_contact_id` via service-role supabase client (non-fatal if writeback fails). DB migration applied second: `_sync_to_resend_audience_internal(uuid, text)` SECDEF helper RPC that reads INTERNAL_FUNCTION_SECRET from Vault, validates action enum, posts to sync-resend-audience Edge Function via pg_net.http_post with x-internal-secret header (best-effort sub-transaction wrap). Then full-body CREATE OR REPLACE of `confirm_newsletter_subscription` and `unsubscribe_from_newsletter` with the TODO comments swapped for `PERFORM public._sync_to_resend_audience_internal(v_subscriber_id, 'add'|'remove')` calls. End-to-end smoke test: created test subscriber row `ebb796a6-cb63-4385-a6df-039aa6c0d71b` at `delivered+g2-smoke-1779563402@resend.dev` (Resend's documented test-delivery address); called `_sync_to_resend_audience_internal(id, 'add')` returned `{dispatched:true, action:'add'}`; pg_net response after 3s showed `{synced:true, action:'add', email:'delivered+g2-smoke-...', resend_contact_id:'e77b7d92-725c-4154-9009-a1cfc3a42a2e'}` — full chain Vault → pg_net → Edge Function → Resend POST → response → contact_id writeback verified; then called same helper with `action='remove'`, returned `{dispatched:true, action:'remove'}`, pg_net response after 3s showed `{synced:true, action:'remove'}`; deleted the smoke-test subscriber row (Resend contact for delivered+g2-smoke-... remains marked unsubscribed in Resend, harmless). (5) **G2.4b SHIPPED — `resend-webhook` Edge Function v3 (strictly-additive extension).** Pulled deployed v2 source via get_edge_function pre-modification per Lovable Credit Conservation Protocol diagnose-before-prescribe. Per Q28.B: does NOT fire `_sync_to_resend_audience_internal` since Resend originated the event and already knows. Wrapped in try/catch — any failure is logged via logStep and swallowed; the 200 ack to Resend is unaffected. (6) **G3 path evaluation: rejected paths documented for closeout.** Path C (vite-plugin-prerender with Puppeteer build-time SSR) drafted in full and sent to Lovable for capability confirmation. Additional Lovable-surfaced impacts that weren't in the original Path C scope: every prerendered page would need a `prerender-ready` event dispatch (~12+ pages, easy to regress); hydration mismatches become a class of production bug the existing pure-SPA doesn't have today (Home.tsx already uses `useState(window.innerWidth)` initializer that would throw during SSR without guard); `react-helmet-async` is not currently installed and adding it requires refactoring the existing inline `document.title`/setMeta pattern across every marketing page; build time goes from seconds to minutes once Puppeteer prerenders ~20 routes per build (compounds as article count grows). Path C-lite (graceful degradation) considered and rejected — "do all the work of Path C and possibly get none of the value" since if Puppeteer fails the build falls back to SPA which is the exact problem we set out to solve. The infrastructure decision (Cloudflare nameserver migration OR Vercel migration OR build-time prerender with smaller scope) gets made once with full context instead of twice in a vacuum. (9) **New standing rule locked Session 94: §135 — Vault secret access in Edge Functions called from SQL via pg_net.** Two distinct secret stores exist with different access patterns: (a) Edge Function Secrets (configured via Supabase Dashboard → Edge Functions → Secrets) are accessed via `Deno.env.get('SECRET_NAME')` inside the Edge Function — fast, synchronous, no DB roundtrip; this is where RESEND_API_KEY and INTERNAL_FUNCTION_SECRET live for direct Edge Function consumption; (b) Vault secrets (`vault.decrypted_secrets`) are accessed via `SELECT decrypted_secret FROM vault.decrypted_secrets WHERE name = '...'` from SQL — slower, requires DB roundtrip, used by SECDEF RPCs that need to call out via pg_net.http_post with a secret in the body or header. Pattern locked Session 94 across `_send_newsletter_confirmation_email_internal`, `subscribe_to_newsletter` (Turnstile siteverify call), `_sync_to_resend_audience_internal`: SECDEF RPC reads secret from Vault, passes to pg_net body or header, Edge Function on the other side reads the same secret from Edge Function Secrets via Deno.env.get and does constant-time safeEqual comparison to verify. **Both stores must be populated when adding a new secret** — adding to Vault only means the SQL side reads it but the Edge Function side gets undefined; adding to Edge Function Secrets only means the Edge Function reads it but SECDEF RPCs that need to pass it through pg_net get NULL from Vault. Three secrets now follow this pattern: INTERNAL_FUNCTION_SECRET (used by every Class B Edge Function + every SECDEF RPC that calls one), CLOUDFLARE_TURNSTILE_SECRET (NEW Session 94 — used by subscribe_to_newsletter RPC posting to Cloudflare siteverify; Vault only since the Edge Function side doesn't consume it), RESEND_API_KEY (used by send-email + sync-resend-audience Edge Functions; Edge Function Secrets only since SQL never touches the Resend API directly). (10) **Cole-side completed Session 94:** Cloudflare Turnstile account provisioned at cloudflare.com (free tier), site key `0x4AAAAAADVBROvQ5jLUUIxJ` (public, embeds in Lovable G6 subscribe form when shipped), secret key added to Supabase Vault as `CLOUDFLARE_TURNSTILE_SECRET` (35 chars, prefix `0x4AAAAAAD` verified). Cole-side verified via pg_net test call to Cloudflare siteverify: real secret + dummy token returned `{"error-codes":["invalid-input-response"],"success":false}` (status 200) confirming Cloudflare accepted the secret as valid then rejected the dummy token. *v100 (SESSION 93 PARTIAL - SUPERSEDED BY v101) - **Session 93 Group G newsletter platform Phase G1 IN PROGRESS — G1.3c shipped clean (state-transition RPCs + 2 audit-shape gap fixes + redundant-index drop + 1 new action_type). G1.3d through G1.5 remaining.**

**G1.3c ship narrative (migration `20260523174208_session93_newsletter_articles_state_transition_rpcs`):**

Single migration, applied + verified. Fixes Session 92 Gaps 1 + 2 + 3 alongside the 5 new state-transition RPCs:

- (1) DROPPED redundant index `newsletter_articles_slug_lookup_idx` (Gap 3 fix; UNIQUE index on slug already handles equality lookups).
- (2) INSERTed new action_type `article_schedule_cancelled` (Q2(B) answer — inverts v2's parsimony default; cancel-schedule and unpublish are now semantically distinct audit events). UPDATEd stale `article_unpublished` description to remove the obsolete "also used for cancel-scheduled" phrasing Session 92 had written.
- (3) `commit_article_version` rewritten with full pre-snapshot state capture per item 15. Asymmetric audit shape per Q1(B): `before_value` carries full article state {slug, title, excerpt, gate, allowed_plan_tiers, status, cover_asset_id, og_image_asset_id, seo fields, authors[]}; `after_value` stays as operation summary {article_id, version_id, version_name}.
- (4) `restore_article_version` same asymmetric fix. Pre-restore state captured BEFORE UPDATE/DELETE/loop runs (critical — author junction is replaced by the restore so before-capture must precede the DELETE). `after_value` carries operation summary + the snapshot authors array.
- (5) NEW `schedule_article(p_article_id, p_publish_at, p_reason)` — status guard `IN ('draft','unpublished')`, terminal-archive guard, p_publish_at skew tolerance (rejects ≤ now() - 1 minute), p_publish_at >now() bump via GREATEST(p_publish_at, now() + interval '1 second') to satisfy the existing scheduled_consistency CHECK constraint when caller's timestamp falls in the `(now() - 1 min, now()]` skew window. Returns `effective_at_clamped` bool so frontend can render "scheduled for now" vs "scheduled for X" appropriately.
- (6) NEW `cancel_scheduled_article(p_article_id, p_reason)` — status guard requires `scheduled`, terminal-archive guard, flips to `draft` and clears `scheduled_for`. Emits new `article_schedule_cancelled` action_type per Q2(B).
- (7) NEW `publish_article(p_article_id, p_reason)` — status guard `IN ('draft','scheduled','unpublished')`, terminal-archive guard, explicit pre-check that gated articles (subscriber_aggregate/plan_tier) have excerpt ≥20 chars (CHECK constraint already enforces this at UPDATE time; explicit guard returns clearer `22023` error vs CHECK's `23514`). Sets status=published, published_at=now(), scheduled_for=NULL. Newsletter dispatch + SSR cache invalidation = bare-comment stubs per Q3(A) — code comments at deferred call sites for G3 + G8 surgical edits.
- (8) NEW `unpublish_article(p_article_id, p_reason)` — status guard requires `published`, terminal-archive guard, flips to `unpublished`. SSR cache invalidation = bare-comment stub.
- (9) NEW `archive_article(p_article_id, p_reason)` — terminal in v1. No double-archive guard. Allows archive from any non-archived status (draft/scheduled/published/unpublished). Sets archived_at=now(). SSR cache invalidation = bare-comment stub.
- (10) All 5 new RPCs: LANGUAGE plpgsql, SECURITY DEFINER, `SET search_path = public, extensions, pg_temp`, gate via `assert_super_admin` + `assert_impersonation_allows('permission_change')` + reason ≥10 chars. REVOKE PUBLIC, GRANT authenticated + service_role. All audit emissions include full before+after JSON with authors array per item 15.

**Lovable approval at G1.3c open:** 3 questions (Q1 audit shape, Q2 schedule_cancelled action_type, Q3 dispatch+cache stub depth) presented with scope-cross-referenced framing and recommendations. Lovable answered Q1=(B), Q2=(B), Q3=(A). Two reinforcements added pre-implementation: (R1) schedule_article skew clamp via GREATEST to satisfy CHECK while preserving 1-minute skew tolerance — answered (B) keep slack and clamp; (R2) archive terminal in v1 — confirmed. Three implementation safeguards added beyond spec: explicit gated-article excerpt pre-check in publish_article (clearer error than CHECK), `effective_at_clamped` return field on schedule_article (frontend signal), permissive archive (from any non-archived status). All three accepted by Cole at draft review.

Re-applied successfully with description added + the stale `article_unpublished` description update bundled in. **Lesson candidate for §131 or new §-number: always query `information_schema.columns` on the target table before drafting any INSERT migration, especially for tables not directly modified in current session's prior work.**

**G1.3d ship narrative (migration `20260523175312_session93_newsletter_articles_read_rpcs`):**

Single migration, applied + verified clean on first try (no aborts this time — pre-migration column-recon discipline applied per lesson candidate from G1.3c apply error). Resolves Session 92 Gap 5 and ships all 5 read RPCs in one atomic migration:

- (1) **Gap 5 resolution: ADD COLUMN `newsletter_subscribers.linked_user_id` (Q4(B) Lovable-locked).** Nullable uuid REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL. Populated at confirm-time when confirming viewer is authenticated; NULL for anon subscribers. Future-proof against users.email rotation. COMMENT documents the multi-subscription edge case for G2 `confirm_newsletter_subscription` to address (when auth.uid() already has a confirmed row: reject or merge — deferred decision).
- (2) **Partial index `newsletter_subscribers_linked_user_id_idx` WHERE `linked_user_id IS NOT NULL AND status = 'confirmed'`** per Lovable R2 reinforcement (status predicate folded into partial index since every read-path query pairs them — smaller index, faster gate check on hot path).
- (3) **`get_article_for_reader(p_slug text)`** — anon-callable SECDEF STABLE, search_path=public,pg_temp. ONE param per v2 N3 (viewer identity from `auth.uid()`). Returns wrapper `{access:'granted'|'paywall'|'not_found', article, authors[, paywall_reason]}` per Lovable R3 vocabulary lock. Gate eval: public always granted; subscriber_aggregate granted if confirmed-subscriber (linked_user_id match OR lower(email) fallback per R1) OR `current_user_active_plan_tier() IS NOT NULL`; plan_tier granted if viewer_tier ∈ allowed_plan_tiers. Paywall payload exactly: `{id, slug, title, excerpt, cover_asset_id, published_at, gate, allowed_plan_tiers}` + `authors` (display-name-only) + `paywall_reason ∈ ('subscriber_required','plan_tier_required')` per R4 contract. NO body_tiptap leakage on paywall. Granted payload carries body_tiptap + full author records (user_id + display_name + order).
- (4) **`preview_article_as_viewer_class(p_article_id uuid, p_viewer_class text)`** — super_admin only (`assert_super_admin` gate, no impersonation gate since read-only). 5-value whitelist (`anon|subscriber|base|premium|individual`). Mirrors `get_article_for_reader` gate-eval logic against simulated viewer state. Echoes `viewer_class` in response so frontend can render "Preview as: [class]" banner. Ignores `published`/`archived` state intentionally (super admin needs to preview drafts and scheduled articles during authoring).
- (5) **`list_articles_for_archive(p_gate_filter text DEFAULT NULL, p_category_id uuid DEFAULT NULL, p_limit integer DEFAULT 12, p_offset integer DEFAULT 0)`** — anon-callable SECDEF STABLE. Q5(A) show-with-previews semantics: returns all published non-archived articles paginated; each row carries `access_state` ∈ `'granted'|'paywall'` per per-viewer gate eval. Wrapper `{items, total, limit, offset}` per §111. Three defenses: (a) `p_gate_filter` whitelist NULL or one-of-3-valid-gates (anti-enumeration per Lovable Q5 followup); (b) `p_limit` clamped via `GREATEST(1, LEAST(p_limit, 50))` per R5 anti-exfiltration cap; (c) `p_category_id` accepted for forward-compat with categories landing in G2/G4 (unused for v1, no error if non-NULL). Single pass viewer-state resolution (subscriber check + plan_tier lookup) once per call, reused across all rows. Paywall row payload byte-identical to `get_article_for_reader` paywall branch per R4.
- (6) **`list_article_versions(p_article_id uuid)`** — super_admin only. Wrapper `{items, total, capped}` per §111. Capped at 200 versions (returns `capped: true` if total > 200; non-blocking, version-history UI in G5 can show "showing latest 200" if hit). Each item: version_id, version_number, version_type, version_name, restored_from_version_id, created_by_user_id, created_by_display_name (left-joined from users), created_at, title_snapshot, body_preview (first 200 chars of `body_tiptap::text` for diff-viewer preview).
- (7) **`get_article_version(p_version_id uuid)`** — super_admin only. Full version row including body_tiptap and metadata_snapshot (which carries the historical authors array per Session 92's _snapshot_article_version pattern).
- (8) GRANTs: get_article_for_reader + list_articles_for_archive to anon + authenticated + service_role (public reader paths). preview + list_versions + get_version to authenticated + service_role (assert_super_admin gates internally). All REVOKE PUBLIC first.

**Lovable approval at G1.3d open:** 2 questions (Q4 subscriber-user linking, Q5 archive gate-filter semantics) with 3-point scope cross-references and recommendations. Lovable confirmed Q4=(B) + Q5=(A) with 5 reinforcements (R1-R5) and 1 question-back about email lowercase enforcement. Question-back answered via DB recon: `newsletter_subscribers_email_lowercase CHECK` already shipped Session 92; subscribers side guaranteed lowercase; users side has no such constraint, so fallback JOIN explicitly lowercases users.email side (R1 honored). One forward-compat note documented: G2 confirm_newsletter_subscription must decide multi-subscription reject-or-merge policy (multi-row edge case in Lovable Q4 point 2). All 5 R1-R5 reinforcements folded into migration body. Three Cole-confirmed implementation calls: preview ignores published/archived state, list_article_versions capped at 200 with capped flag, all author display_name reads use `users.full_name`.

**G1.3e ship narrative (migration `20260523175845_session93_newsletter_draft_pruning_function_and_cron`):**

Single migration applying:
- (1) `prune_newsletter_draft_versions()` zero-arg SECDEF plpgsql function, search_path=public,pg_temp. Per article: identify draft version rows older than 7 days, rank `ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY article_id ORDER BY created_at DESC)`, DELETE rows where rn > 20 (keeping top-20-most-recent per article). Non-draft version types (named_revision/scheduled/published/restored_from) retained forever. Returns wrapper `{deleted_count, articles_touched, ran_at}` for cron observability. REVOKE PUBLIC, GRANT service_role + postgres.
- (2) Cron job `prune_newsletter_draft_versions` registered at `35 6 * * *` (non-colliding slot per Session 92 Discovery 2). **Shipped DISABLED** (`active = false`) per Lovable v2 item 3 — Cole monitors draft accumulation for 2 weeks before enabling. Comment in migration documents the enable command (`SELECT cron.alter_job(jobid, active := true)`).

**Apply error caught + corrected (second such error this session):** First apply attempt failed at `UPDATE cron.job SET active = false WHERE jobname = '...'` with `42501 permission denied for table job`. The migration role doesn't own `cron.job` directly. Re-applied successfully using `cron.schedule_in_database(name, schedule, command, database, username, active)` which has an `active boolean` parameter — registers the job in disabled state in a single function call without needing direct UPDATE on `cron.job`. **Lesson candidate for §-number at session close: pg_cron migrations must use `cron.schedule_in_database()` for disable-at-ship pattern, never follow-up `UPDATE cron.job`. The function API has appropriate permissions; the table-level UPDATE does not.** Pairs with the G1.3c lesson candidate (always query schema before INSERT). Both are recon-discipline rules.

**Smoke test:** Single zero-arg call to `prune_newsletter_draft_versions()` against currently-empty `newsletter_article_versions` table. Returns `{ran_at: <timestamp>, deleted_count: 0, articles_touched: 0}`. Confirms function callable end-to-end with correct wrapper shape, no permission errors, no SECDEF issues. Cron job remains active=false; no scheduled run will occur until Cole enables. No new audit rows (function emits no log_super_admin_action — it's an internal maintenance cron, not a super-admin action).

**EXACT STATE OF DB AT END OF SESSION 93 G1.3e:**
- Tables, RLS, action_types, indexes: unchanged from G1.3d close.
- Functions: +1 new = 20 newsletter-related functions total.
- Cron jobs: +1 new (`prune_newsletter_draft_versions` at 35 6 * * *, active=false). First newsletter cron job to ship. Two more (`prune_newsletter_subscribe_attempts` at 6:15, `expire_pending_newsletter_confirmations` at 6:25) owed in G2.

**G1.4 ship narrative — TWO migrations applied this phase (the second a fix-up for whitelist omission caught by smoke):**

**Migration 1: `20260523181119_session93_newsletter_articles_inline_asset_refs`** (748 lines)

**Lovable approval at G1.4 open:** Q6 raised with three coherent paths (A bucket-only, B content_assets-integrated, C hybrid) plus four implementation sub-questions (Q6.1-Q6.4). Pre-Lovable recon discovered: (a) existing `_walk_block_config_for_asset_refs` walker is structurally lesson_block-only and can't be surgically extended for TipTap (handoff/scope assumed it could); (b) v2 spec for `convert-html-to-tiptap` Edge Function had inline images going straight to Storage bypassing `content_assets` — meaning scope's "extend content_asset_refs to 7-way" assumed an integration that wasn't fully specified. Cole locked path (B): inline images flow through `content_assets` with `attrs.asset_id` as canonical TipTap node reference, never `src`. Lovable confirmed Q6.1-Q6.4 + 5 reinforcements + 1 question-back (FK setup on `content_asset_refs.asset_id`). Recon confirmed FK is `ON DELETE RESTRICT`, archive flows are soft via `archived_at`, mirroring `_cascade_archive_asset_refs_for_content_item` is correct.

**What landed in migration 1:**

- (1) Schema extension: ADD COLUMN `content_asset_refs.newsletter_article_id uuid REFERENCES newsletter_articles(id) ON DELETE CASCADE`. DROP + recreate `content_asset_refs_exactly_one_parent` CHECK as 7-way. Partial index `WHERE newsletter_article_id IS NOT NULL AND archived_at IS NULL`.
- (2) `_walk_tiptap_for_image_asset_refs(p_body_tiptap jsonb)` — recursive CTE over TipTap node tree. Returns `TABLE(out_ref_path text, out_asset_id uuid)`. Image nodes with `attrs.asset_id` matching UUID pattern → emit row with path like `body.image[2.1]`. Image nodes with missing/non-uuid asset_id → silently skipped (per Lovable R-Q6.2a). Walker name encodes v1 scope per Lovable R-Q6.3.
- (3) `_cascade_archive_asset_refs_for_newsletter_article(p_article_id, p_caller_id, p_archive_reason)` — exact mirror of `_cascade_archive_asset_refs_for_content_item` adapted to newsletter parent. Archives refs first, then for each affected non-library asset where `_asset_active_ref_count = 0`, archives the asset via `_archive_asset_internal`.
- (4) `_rebind_newsletter_article_asset_refs(p_article_id, p_caller_id)` — Rebind owns ALL article refs (cover + og + inline). Three sources, one function. Phase 1 builds desired-set from cover_asset_id column + og_image_asset_id column + walker output; for each desired ref does FK-safety pre-check (skip with NOTICE if asset not active per Lovable R-Q6.2b) then B-2 rebind on `(asset_id, newsletter_article_id, archived_at IS NULL)` UPDATE-or-INSERT. Phase 2 archives refs whose asset_id is no longer in desired set. Returns `{refs_created, refs_rebound, refs_archived}`.
- (5) Integration into 4 existing RPCs (full function body replacements via CREATE OR REPLACE):
  - `upsert_article`: rebind call BEFORE audit emission per Lovable R-Q6.4. Audit `after_value` includes `asset_refs` summary.
  - `auto_save_article`: rebind call after UPDATE; no audit to coordinate with.
  - `restore_article_version`: rebind BEFORE audit emission; `after_value` includes `asset_refs`.
  - `archive_article`: cascade-archive call BEFORE audit emission. **Fixes §43 gap from G1.3c**: original archive_article shipped without cascade integration. Migration body comment calls this out explicitly.

**Migration 2: `session93_newsletter_articles_inline_asset_refs_archive_reason_whitelist`** (fix-up)

**Apply error caught by smoke test (third such error this session):** G1.4 migration 1 shipped clean (`success: true`). Smoke test then failed at T7 (archive_article cascade) with `23514 content_assets_archive_reason_check` violation. The CHECK constraint whitelists 8 archive_reason values; my cascade function passed `'newsletter_article_archived'` which was not in the whitelist. Same §99 discipline that applies to action_types: every flow that writes to a whitelisted column must add its value in the same migration. Re-applied as fix-up migration 2, extending the whitelist to 9 values.

**Lesson candidate for §-number at session close (third recon-discipline rule this session, all related):** ALL of these belong to the same family — query the schema/constraint state before drafting any migration that writes whitelisted values, calls cron-restricted functions, or INSERTs into tables not freshly authored. The pattern across all three:

- G1.3c apply error: missed NOT NULL `description` column on `super_admin_action_types` INSERT
- G1.3e apply error: tried to UPDATE `cron.job` table (no permission); needed `cron.schedule_in_database(active => false)`
- G1.4 smoke error: missed whitelist update on `content_assets.archive_reason` CHECK

All three preventable by pre-migration recon. Standing rule candidate: **"Before drafting any migration that INSERTs/UPDATEs/calls into a table not freshly authored in the current session, query the schema first (information_schema.columns for nullability/defaults, pg_constraint for CHECK predicates, pg_proc for available functions)."**

**Smoke test (G1.4 full lifecycle, 8 invariants):**

Fixture: 1 article, 1 library asset (cover), 2 throwaway non-library assets (inline body images). Tests:

- T1: Create article with cover + 2 inline images → 3 active refs total. PASS.
- T2: Rebind result reports `refs_created=3`. PASS.
- T3: `ref_field` paths correct: `cover_asset`, `body.image[1]`, `body.image[2.1]`. PASS.
- T4: Edit body to remove second inline image → 2 active refs + 1 archived ref. PASS.
- T5: Rebind result reports `refs_archived=1`. PASS.
- T6: Idempotent re-save (same body) → `refs_rebound=2, refs_created=0` (B-2 rebind preserves rows, no churn). PASS.
- T7: Archive article → cascade archives 2 remaining refs + non-library asset_a (only ref archived); library cover asset stays active (protected by `is_library_asset = true` filter). PASS.
- T8: Walker tolerance — body with 3 image nodes (1 with `src` only, 1 with non-uuid asset_id, 1 with valid uuid) → only 1 ref created, malformed nodes silently skipped. PASS.

6 new audit rows from smoke (article_created + article_saved×2 + article_archived×2 + 1 more — covering both fixture article and tolerance article lifecycle). All reason-prefixed `'G1.4 smoke test - ...'`. Fixture cascade verified: library asset remained active, non-library throwaway assets correctly archived.

- 4 Lovable approval cycles: Q1-Q3 (G1.3c audit shape + new action_type + dispatch stub), Q4-Q5 (G1.3d subscriber linking + archive semantics), Q6 (G1.4 inline image asset model — biggest design call of the session; scope-redesign moment when recon revealed `_walk_block_config_for_asset_refs` couldn't be surgically extended).
- 0 Lovable code cycles this session (all backend; no frontend prompts written).
- Phase G1 backend lift COMPLETE. Session 94 opens on Phase G2 (subscriber email flow + Resend audience sync + Cloudflare Turnstile + public subscribe/confirm/unsubscribe RPCs).

**§-numbered standing rule candidates from Session 93 (Cole locks at session close in architecture-reference v96 entry):**

- §129 candidate from Session 92: SECDEF functions calling pgcrypto must include `extensions` in search_path
- §130 candidate from Session 92: Smoke-test audit rows are unavoidable + must be self-identifying via reason prefix
- §131 candidate from Session 92: pg_cron slot collision discovery before scheduling new jobs
- **§132 candidate from Session 93 (NEW):** Pre-migration schema recon discipline — before drafting any migration that INSERTs/UPDATEs/calls into a table not freshly authored in current session, query (a) `information_schema.columns` for nullability/defaults, (b) `pg_constraint` for CHECK predicates, (c) `pg_proc` for available function signatures. Caught 3 apply errors in Session 93 alone; all preventable.
- **§133 candidate from Session 93 (NEW):** TipTap node asset reference contract — newsletter inline image nodes MUST carry `attrs.asset_id` referencing a `content_assets` row; `src` is derived at render time, never canonical. Locks Lovable's Q6.2 architecture decision into a discoverable rule for future authors (G2 Edge Function, G4 native upload, G6 reader render path all honor this).
- **§134 candidate from Session 93 (NEW):** pg_cron disable-at-ship pattern — use `cron.schedule_in_database(name, schedule, command, database, username, active => false)` rather than `cron.schedule()` + `UPDATE cron.job SET active = false`. The UPDATE path requires elevated permissions not available to migration roles; the function API has appropriate permissions.

Native TipTap editor toolbar: bold, italic, underline (off by default), strikethrough, inline code, H2/H3/H4 (H1 reserved for article title at template level), bulleted+numbered lists, link, blockquote, image upload, embed (YouTube/Vimeo URL), code block (lowlight syntax highlighting), horizontal rule, undo/redo. Deferred to v2: tables, footnotes, custom callouts, drop caps/pull quotes, author-uploaded native video.

**Lovable v2 review nits resolved at migration-write time (3 of 3):**
- N1 (`pgcrypto` schema-qualification): VERIFIED `pgcrypto` v1.3 installed in `extensions` schema (not `public`). Confirmed via `pg_extension` query before any migration ran. Pattern locked: SECDEF functions calling `digest()` or `gen_random_bytes()` use `SET search_path = public, extensions, pg_temp`. No `CREATE EXTENSION` line needed. Applied in G1.2b (import_newsletter_subscribers_bulk uses both digest and gen_random_bytes).
- N2 (CHECK constraint placement + tier allowlist): All CHECK constraints written as named `CONSTRAINT name CHECK (...)` clauses at end of column list. Added `newsletter_articles_allowed_tiers_valid_values CHECK (allowed_plan_tiers <@ ARRAY['base','premium','individual']::text[])` — array-subset operator prevents garbage tier strings.
- N3 (drop `p_viewer_user_id` footgun): Confirmed at design time, will be reflected in G1.3d when `get_article_for_reader` is written (NOT yet shipped). Signature will be `get_article_for_reader(p_slug text)` — viewer identity always from `auth.uid()`. `preview_article_as_viewer_class` becomes the only way for super-admin to simulate different viewer.

**Pre-migration architectural discoveries Session 92:**
- `pgcrypto` v1.3 lives in `extensions` schema (not `public`). pg_cron v1.6.4 lives in `pg_catalog`. pg_net v0.20.0 lives in `extensions`.
- Existing precedent for digest()/gen_random_bytes() calls is mixed: `corporate_employee_choose_individual` uses `search_path=public, extensions, auth`; `peer_access_request_create` uses `search_path=public` (risky — relies on default search_path resolving extensions). NEW pattern locked for G1 onward: explicit `extensions` in search_path.
- Existing pg_cron job COLLISION at slot `20 6 * * *`: `process_due_scheduled_assignments_daily` already runs at 6:20 (touches scheduled_assignments, user_curriculum_assignments, user_module_assignments, coach_certifications, coach_mentor_assignments, super_admin_audit_log). Newsletter cron jobs rescheduled to NON-colliding minutes: `prune_newsletter_subscribe_attempts` at 6:15, `expire_pending_newsletter_confirmations` at 6:25, `prune_newsletter_draft_versions` at 6:35. Working sets are disjoint (newsletter_* tables only), no shared lock contention with assignments cron.
- `super_admin_audit_log` has an immutability trigger `block_audit_log_mutations()` that blocks UPDATE and DELETE. Smoke-test audit rows persist permanently. Convention adopted: all smoke-test RPC calls use `reason` prefix `"G1.X smoke test - <detail>"` so test rows are self-identifying. Five smoke-test audit rows remain in production audit log after Session 92 (acceptable — they're correctly labeled).
- `super_admin_audit_log.action_type` has HARD FK to `super_admin_action_types.action_type`. Confirms §99 discipline: action_types MUST be INSERTed in same migration as RPCs that emit them, BEFORE the RPC body can be called. Verified at deploy time — every G1 migration that adds RPCs emitting new action_types INSERTs those action_types in the same migration.
- JWT context test pattern: `set_config('request.jwt.claims', json_build_object(...)::text, false)` for session-local context (true is transaction-local and breaks across MCP statements). Used in DO blocks for multi-step smoke tests.
- `current_user_account_type()` reads `auth.uid()` directly — has `SET search_path TO 'public', 'auth', 'pg_temp'`, SECURITY DEFINER, STABLE.
- `assert_super_admin()` raises 42501 with message `'Permission denied: caller is not a BrainWise super admin'` when `current_user_account_type() IS DISTINCT FROM 'brainwise_super_admin'`.
- `assert_impersonation_allows(p_action_category)` denylist includes `permission_change` for `account_type` modifications. Newsletter authoring RPCs use `permission_change` as the action category (treated as content-management surface; the denylist behavior is appropriate — impersonating a super admin shouldn't allow article authoring under their identity).
- `log_super_admin_action(p_target_user_id, p_target_org_id, p_action_type, p_before, p_after, p_reason, p_mode)` is the canonical audit insert path. Returns the inserted audit row id (uuid). Implements scheduled-assignment-actor GUC bypass for cron context.

(5) **`20260523171529_session92_newsletter_articles_write_rpcs`** APPLIED + VERIFIED (with known gap — see FOLLOW-UPS). Creates 5 SECURITY DEFINER functions, all `SET search_path = public, extensions, pg_temp`:
   - **`_snapshot_article_version(p_article_id uuid, p_version_type text, p_version_name text DEFAULT NULL, p_restored_from_version_id uuid DEFAULT NULL) RETURNS uuid`** — internal helper. Loads article, builds authors jsonb via `jsonb_agg(jsonb_build_object('user_id', author_user_id, 'order', author_order) ORDER BY author_order)` per Lovable v2 item 7, builds metadata_snapshot with `{authors, gate, allowed_plan_tiers, cover_asset_id, og_image_asset_id, seo_title, seo_description, canonical_url, source_type, word_count, read_time_minutes}`, computes next version_number, INSERTs row, returns version id. REVOKE PUBLIC, GRANT service_role only (NOT authenticated — only callable from other SECDEF RPCs and service_role).
   - **`auto_save_article(p_article_id, p_body_tiptap, + 7 optional metadata DEFAULT NULL params) RETURNS jsonb`** — silent auto-save per Lovable v2 item 3. Gate: assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows('permission_change'). Touches body + curated metadata subset only (NOT gate/authors/status/scheduling/cover/og_image/source_type). UPDATE uses COALESCE so NULL params preserve existing values. Calls `_snapshot_article_version(_, 'draft', NULL, NULL)`. **DOES NOT call log_super_admin_action — no audit row.** GRANTed authenticated + service_role.
   - **`upsert_article(17 params) RETURNS jsonb`** — explicit save (create or update). Gate: assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows('permission_change') + reason ≥10 chars. Branches on `p_article_id IS NULL` → create with `article_created` audit, else update with `article_saved` audit. At create, defaults `p_author_user_ids` to `[caller]` if NULL or empty. At update, captures before_value with authors array via jsonb_agg (per Lovable v2 item 15). If `p_author_user_ids IS NOT NULL`: validates cardinality ≥ 1, DELETEs all current author rows for the article, INSERTs new rows with `author_order = idx`. Captures after_value with authors. Calls `_snapshot_article_version(_, 'draft', NULL, NULL)`. Audit row written via log_super_admin_action with full before/after JSONs. GRANTed authenticated + service_role.
   - **`commit_article_version(p_article_id, p_version_name, p_reason) RETURNS jsonb`** — Gate: assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows + reason ≥10 + non-empty version_name. Calls `_snapshot_article_version(_, 'named_revision', p_version_name, NULL)`. Audit row written. **GAP: `before_value = NULL` on the audit row, `after_value` contains only `{article_id, version_id, version_name}`. Does NOT include current article state with authors for auditor reconstruction. Inconsistent with Lovable v2 item 15 discipline — FOLLOW-UP for next session.**
   - **`restore_article_version(p_version_id, p_reason) RETURNS jsonb`** — Gate: assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows + reason ≥10. Loads version row. Validates `metadata_snapshot.authors` is non-empty array (raises 22023 if missing). UPDATEs article body + metadata fields from snapshot. DELETEs current author rows. Loops `jsonb_array_elements(authors)` from snapshot, INSERTs new author junction rows per Lovable v2 Q-A (restoring brings back historical author roster even if those users have since lost super_admin status). Calls `_snapshot_article_version(_, 'restored_from', NULL, p_version_id)`. Audit row written. **GAP: `before_value = NULL` on audit row. Should include pre-restore article state with authors. FOLLOW-UP for next session.**
   - Verification PASSED end-to-end on smoke article slug `g1-3b-smoke-test-article` (id `78a8a0c5-ea5f-445e-92b3-2246f6793180` — now DELETEd, cascade clean): create → commit named revision → auto-save (silent, NO audit row created) → explicit upsert (article_saved audit created with both before_value.authors AND after_value.authors populated per item 15) → restore to named revision. Final article state confirmed body + title + word_count rolled back to v2 (named_revision) snapshot. Version sequence: v1=draft, v2=named_revision (name 'First named revision'), v3=draft (from auto_save), v4=draft (from upsert), v5=restored_from (with restored_from_version_id pointing at v2). All 5 versions had `metadata_snapshot.authors` populated with `[{order:0, user_id:1d14e510...}]`. Smoke-article DELETE cascade clean (0 articles, 0 authors, 0 versions remaining). 4 smoke-test audit rows remain (article_created, article_version_committed, article_saved, article_restored_from_version, all reason-prefixed 'G1.3b smoke test - ...').

**MIGRATIONS NOT YET APPLIED — REMAINING G1 WORK FOR NEXT SESSION (in order):**

(A) **`session92_newsletter_articles_state_transition_rpcs`** (G1.3c) — Create 5 RPCs: `schedule_article(p_article_id, p_publish_at, p_reason)`, `cancel_scheduled_article(p_article_id, p_reason)`, `publish_article(p_article_id, p_reason)`, `unpublish_article(p_article_id, p_reason)`, `archive_article(p_article_id, p_reason)`. All SECURITY DEFINER, search_path=public,extensions,pg_temp, gate via assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows('permission_change') + reason ≥10. publish_article must trigger background dispatch via pg_net.http_post to `dispatch-newsletter-article` Edge Function (lands G8) for gated articles — for v1 just log the intent and return; the actual Edge Function ships in G8. publish/unpublish/archive must invalidate SSR cache (lands G3). For G1.3c, just write the state transitions + audit rows; cache invalidation and dispatch trigger are stubs returning success. **Per item 15 discipline: capture before_value with full article state including authors on EVERY audit emission. Apply this discipline to commit_article_version and restore_article_version (see FOLLOW-UP below) in the same migration to fix the gap from G1.3b.**

(B) **`session92_newsletter_articles_read_rpcs`** (G1.3d) — Create 5 read RPCs:
   - `get_article_for_reader(p_slug text) RETURNS jsonb` — anon-callable SECDEF. Drops `p_viewer_user_id` param per Lovable v2 N3. Viewer identity always via `auth.uid()`. Resolves subscriber status via JOIN to users.email (NOTE: this requires the user to have signed up for newsletter using the same email as their account — confirm UX flow in G2; alternative is matching on user_id directly if subscribers table gets a `linked_user_id` column). Returns `{access:'granted', article, authors}` or `{access:'paywall', article:{id,slug,title,excerpt,cover_asset_id,published_at,gate,allowed_plan_tiers?}, authors, paywall_reason:'subscriber_required'|'plan_tier_required'}`. The 3-state gate evaluation: public always granted; subscriber_aggregate granted if confirmed_subscriber OR `current_user_active_plan_tier() IS NOT NULL`; plan_tier granted if `current_user_active_plan_tier() = ANY(allowed_plan_tiers)`. Anon and authenticated grants.
   - `preview_article_as_viewer_class(p_article_id uuid, p_viewer_class text) RETURNS jsonb` — super_admin only, simulates `get_article_for_reader` output for given viewer class (`'anon'`, `'subscriber'`, `'base'`, `'premium'`, `'individual'`). Reimplements gate logic against simulated viewer state — does NOT modify DB.
   - `list_articles_for_archive(p_gate_filter text DEFAULT NULL, p_category_id uuid DEFAULT NULL, p_limit integer DEFAULT 12, p_offset integer DEFAULT 0) RETURNS jsonb` — anon-callable. Returns published articles respecting gate (anon sees public only with full body; auth-no-sub sees public + subscriber_aggregate previews; auth-subscriber sees public + subscriber_aggregate full + plan_tier previews; plan-tier holders see all). Wrapper shape `{items, total, limit, offset}` per §111 type discipline.
   - `list_article_versions(p_article_id uuid) RETURNS jsonb` — super_admin only. Returns `{items: [{version_id, version_number, version_type, version_name, restored_from_version_id, created_by_user_id, created_at, body_preview_first_200_chars}]}`.
   - `get_article_version(p_version_id uuid) RETURNS jsonb` — super_admin only. Returns full version row including body_tiptap and metadata_snapshot.

(C) **`session92_newsletter_draft_pruning_function_and_cron`** (G1.3e) — Create `prune_newsletter_draft_versions()` function per Lovable v2 item 3 retention: per article, identify draft versions older than 7 days, rank by created_at DESC, keep top 20, delete the rest. Register pg_cron job `prune_newsletter_draft_versions` at `35 6 * * *` (non-colliding slot per Session 92 discovery). Test by inserting fixture draft rows >7 days old, running function manually, confirming top-20 retention. **Cron schedule can ship disabled initially — Cole monitors draft accumulation for 2 weeks before flipping cron on.** Document the disable/enable toggle in the migration.

DROP CONSTRAINT `content_asset_refs_exactly_one_parent` (current 6-way), ADD CONSTRAINT with 7-way CASE-WHEN. CREATE INDEX `content_asset_refs_newsletter_article_idx` (partial WHERE newsletter_article_id IS NOT NULL). **FOLLOW-UP FIXES OWED IN G1.3c (not blocking next session start):**
- `commit_article_version` should populate `before_value` with full article state including authors before the snapshot completes. Currently writes `before_value = NULL`. Inconsistent with Lovable v2 item 15. Fix in G1.3c migration by adding a "capture pre-snapshot state" block at the top of the function using the same pattern as `upsert_article`.
- `restore_article_version` same gap. Currently writes `before_value = NULL`. Fix in G1.3c by capturing pre-restore state (current article body + authors) before the UPDATE.
- `newsletter_articles_slug_lookup_idx` is REDUNDANT with `newsletter_articles_slug_unique` (the UNIQUE constraint creates a unique btree index that handles slug lookups). Drop the redundant index in G1.3c or G1.3e migration. Both are non-blocking; production usage will pick the unique index automatically.

**ARCHITECTURE NOTES FROM SESSION 92 (consider for next architecture-reference version §-numbered rule):**
- Pattern candidate (§129): SECDEF functions calling pgcrypto functions (digest, gen_random_bytes) must `SET search_path = public, extensions, pg_temp` because pgcrypto lives in `extensions` schema in Supabase. Skipping `extensions` works only if extensions schema is in the default search_path before SECDEF locks it — risky pattern (`peer_access_request_create` precedent does this and works today but is fragile to future search_path policy changes). Explicit inclusion is the safe pattern.
- Pattern candidate (§130): Smoke-test audit rows are unavoidable when testing super_admin RPCs because `super_admin_audit_log` is immutable (`block_audit_log_mutations` trigger). Convention: all smoke-test RPC calls prefix `p_reason` with `'G<phase>.<step> smoke test - <detail>'` so test rows are self-identifying. Five such rows added Session 92, all correctly labeled.
- Pattern candidate (§131): pg_cron job slot collision discovery via `SELECT jobname, schedule FROM cron.job` BEFORE planning new job schedules. Existing `process_due_scheduled_assignments_daily` at `20 6 * * *` would have collided with Session 92 originally-planned newsletter slots; rescheduled to 6:15/6:25/6:35. Discipline: query cron.job first when adding cron-driven features.

- AIRSA facet-interpretation gap, messaging subsystem, module reorder gap, MFA trusted-device feature, editor thumbnail-loss-on-republish hardening, coach-paid invitation email verification, `create-checkout` graceful-degradation hardening, AIRSA Phases 3e-8, SOC 2 written policies, Action-Oriented Voice Redesign, pricing-reads refactor, corporate contract renewal schema change, Clarity Engine, Session 71 anon EXECUTE audit, post-launch `coach_clients_client_view` SECDEF refactor, `results_available` NAI/AIRSA/HSS coverage, `users.last_active_at` infrastructure, `user_ui_preferences` dedicated table migration, bulk Phase 11 v2, /super-admin/coaches consolidation, Members Surface v2 polish, button labeling pattern, legacy 2-arg `search_impersonation_targets` cleanup, Mentor Portal v2 MQ-1 through MQ-4.

(7) **One new standing rule locked Session 89:** **§128 — Radix Collapsible state-driven child visibility requires `className="group"` on Root + `group-data-[state=X]:hidden` on children.** Discovered during Cycle B Lovable Pass 2 review. The bare `data-[state=X]:hidden` Tailwind variant reads the state from the element it's applied to, NOT from a Radix parent — so a child of Collapsible.Root marked `data-[state=open]:hidden` would silently fail to hide when the parent opens (the child has no state attribute of its own). The correct pattern mirrors the navigation-menu.tsx codebase precedent: `<Collapsible className="group">` propagates a `group` marker that lets descendants use `group-data-[state=X]:hidden` to read the Radix state from the marked ancestor. Without the marker, child visibility silently does nothing. Concrete: Cycle B's iteration history rendering uses `<Collapsible defaultOpen={isLatest} className="group">` with `<div className="text-sm ... group-data-[state=open]:hidden">` for the preview-in-Root pattern (preview visible when Collapsible is CLOSED, hidden when OPEN; full content rendered inside CollapsibleContent only when OPEN). Caught in plan-mode Pass 2 review before ship. (8) **DEFERRED items added Session 89:** **Mentor Portal v2 build queue (MQ-1 through MQ-4)**: keyboard-driven review queue (j/k navigation between submitted-for-review items), rubric-based scoring on SkillsPracticeReviewPanel (numeric 1-5 per criterion with weighted average displayed to trainee), timestamped media annotations (drop comments at specific timestamps in submitted video/audio), AI-assisted feedback suggestions via Anthropic API (mentor types initial reaction, AI proposes 2-3 elaborated feedback drafts mentor can pick or refine). All non-blocking, all "phase 2+ when usage data informs prioritization." **Cycle C cosmetic follow-ups (3 items rolled into a single Session 90 mini-cycle)**: MessageSquare → FileText (or Library) icon swap in AppSidebar for "Feedback Templates" entry to eliminate AI Chat icon collision; FeedbackTemplates.tsx h1 font-semibold → font-bold for NotificationSettings consistency; FeedbackTemplatePicker loading state regain `role="status"` + `aria-label="Loading templates"` attributes (single-line a11y fix). (9) **Carried forward unchanged to Session 90.** Phase 10 polish queue remaining: Round 7 (Coach surfaces — CoachClients/ClientResults/CoachInvoices; CoachInvoices touched Round 1 palette work, CoachClients touched Session 85 Bug 1, ClientResults touched Session 85 Bugs 4+5; all three have had narrow patches but not full polish passes). Then formal Group C closure. All other Session 88 deferred items unchanged (AIRSA facet-interpretation gap, messaging subsystem, module reorder gap, MFA trusted-device, editor thumbnail hardening, create-checkout graceful-degradation, coach-paid invitation email verification, AIRSA Phases 3e-8, SOC 2 written policies, Action-Oriented Voice Redesign, pricing-reads refactor, corporate contract renewal schema, Clarity Engine, Session 71 anon EXECUTE audit, post-launch coach_clients_client_view SECDEF refactor, results_available NAI/AIRSA/HSS coverage, Members Surface v2 polish 5 items, button labeling pattern inconsistency, legacy 2-arg search_impersonation_targets cleanup, users.last_active_at infrastructure, user_ui_preferences dedicated table migration, bulk role change / MFA reset / password reset / send message Phase 11 v2, /super-admin/coaches consolidation evaluation). (10) **NEW standing rules locked Session 88.** **§125 — Adding optional params to existing PL/pgSQL functions requires DROP-then-CREATE, not CREATE-OR-REPLACE.** `CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION` only replaces functions with identical argument signatures. Adding a new optional param creates a NEW function and leaves the old in place. PostgreSQL then has two overloads with overlapping named-args sets, and PostgREST's overload resolution becomes ambiguous when a call comes in with the original arg count (planner cannot choose between exact match on old vs default-fill on new). Correct sequence: (a) CREATE OR REPLACE with new signature including optional param DEFAULT NULL — creates the new function alongside the old; (b) test new function in isolation; (c) DROP FUNCTION old signature RESTRICT — RESTRICT fails loud if anything depends on the old signature; CASCADE would silently chain into views or triggers, never use it for this pattern; (d) re-test: existing N-named-arg callers resolve to (N+1)-arg via default fill. Skipping step (c) leaves intermittent `42725 is not unique` errors at runtime. Pairs with §96 (CHECK constraint audit on RPC validation changes) — both reinforce that PostgreSQL function evolution touches multiple layers atomically. **§126 — Lovable can ship adjacent backend changes when load-bearing.** During cycle 1, Lovable proactively extended `search_impersonation_targets` from the existing 3-arg form to a 14-arg form to fix the directMember query bug — outside the prompt's stated frontend-only scope but minimum-coupled correct fix for the bug. Accepted. Pattern locked: future cycles include explicit "DO NOT modify any RPC" guardrail in frontend-only Lovable prompts where backend ownership must stay with Claude (e.g., when Lovable lacks Supabase MCP write access in the specific session, or when backward-compat verification is critical). When Lovable is permitted to ship adjacent backend, the prompt explicitly authorizes it and lists the exact RPC names that may be touched. Don't trust prompt-scope discipline alone to prevent adjacent edits — call out what's allowed and what isn't. **§127 — Caller-owns-mutation + description slot for multi-step modals reusing single-step primitives.** When a complex action surface (multi-target picker + extra fields + amber inline gate hint) needs to reuse an existing single-step primitive (JustifiedActionDialog), pass the multi-step content through the dialog's `description: React.ReactNode` slot rather than building a parallel multi-step dialog. The dialog primitive renders description content inside a `<p>` (shadcn DialogDescription wraps in `<p>`), so the multi-step content must use `<span className="block">` wrappers — NOT `<div>` — to avoid invalid HTML nesting and the React hydration warning that follows. Throw-then-mapError pattern for non-reason validation: the multi-step content sets state outside the dialog, and the dialog's `onSubmit` callback (which gets the reason string) reads that state and throws a typed error if any pre-condition isn't met; `mapError` translates the thrown error to user-facing copy. Concrete example: 11.D.2's MemberDrawerAssignments uses 4 launcher components, each wrapping JustifiedActionDialog with its own target picker + due date + amber inline gate hint rendered inside the description slot. (11) **DEFERRED Build Queue items added Session 88 (v2 polish for Members surface):** (a) **Members Surface v2 Polish — 5 deferred audit findings.** Mobile column-hiding refinement based on real analytics (current ladder is best-guess; revisit after collecting mobile super-admin usage data). Row hover-reveal opacity pattern keyboard discoverability (current: `opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100`; keyboard users can't trigger hover so the action button is invisible until they Tab to it). Mentor body text contrast bump from 4.79:1 marginal to 7:1+. Filter chip horizontal scroll on narrow viewports (currently wraps vertical, pushes table down). Page header "Bulk Import" + "Schedule" button stacking polish at narrow widths. (b) **Inconsistent button labeling pattern** (Toggle Sidebar, Log Out, drawer Close use label-on-inner-span instead of `aria-label` on button itself). Works functionally but inconsistent with rest of codebase. (c) **Legacy 2-arg `search_impersonation_targets(p_query, p_limit) -> 6-col` overload still live** — cycle 1.5 dropped only the 14-arg; the 2-arg remains because it has a non-overlapping named-args set with the canonical 15-arg. The 4 legacy callsites (Users.tsx + LearningAdmin.tsx 3 sites) were deleted in 11.D so the overload is dead code in the production app surface but still callable from psql. Default filter: Status=Active. Saved views with per-user persistence. Search: email + name + org (current `search_impersonation_targets` scope unchanged). Typeahead 250ms debounce min 2 chars composes with filters with match highlighting. (6) **Phase 11.B backend — 5 migrations applied + verified.** All five live on production. **M1 `add_users_ui_preferences_column`**: `ALTER TABLE public.users ADD COLUMN ui_preferences jsonb NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb;` + COMMENT documenting write-whole-read-whole contract. Smoke test passed: round-trip write+read+restore via `||` jsonb concatenation operator works cleanly. **M2 `extend_search_impersonation_targets`**: DROP RESTRICT then CREATE on 3-arg form → new 14-arg signature with 7 new returned columns (`is_mentor`, `active_assignment_count`, `certification_count`, `worst_certification_status`, `account_status`, `last_sign_in_at` from auth.users via SECDEF, `show_coach_tab`) and 11 new optional filter+sort params (all NULL-default so existing 4 callsites unchanged). Active assignment count = sum of active user_curriculum_assignments + active user_module_assignments + coach_mentor_assignments where trainee_user_id=u.id AND ended_at IS NULL (trainee side, not mentor side). worst_certification_status priority: revoked > in_progress > certified. Sort columns supported: name / email / account_type / organization / account_status / worst_certification_status / active_assignments / certification_count / last_login. Smoke tests passed: real cbastian search returns 3 rows with all new columns populated (Cole: is_mentor=true, active_assignment_count=1, certification_count=2, worst_certification_status='in_progress', show_coach_tab=true; Test Coach: show_coach_tab=true from account_type='coach'; Test Client 3: show_coach_tab=false individual account_type); filter by is_mentor=true returns 3 mentors (Cole + Test Coach Cert + Test Coach 1, matching audit count); composability (search 'test' + p_account_types=['coach'] + sort by name DESC) works correctly. `auth.users.last_sign_in_at` accessible via SECDEF; postgres role has SELECT on auth.users (verified by population in returned column). **M3 `create_list_user_audit_history_rpc`**: New SECDEF RPC `list_user_audit_history(p_user_id, p_limit=50, p_offset=0, p_categories[]=NULL)`. Returns audit_id, created_at, action_type, computed category (via CASE on action_type — role/completion/certification/permission/impersonation/other), actor_user_id, actor_name with 'Unknown admin' fallback for null actor_user_id, actor_email, actor_account_type, reason, before_value, after_value, detail, total_count via COUNT(*) OVER(). Smoke test on Cole returned 2 entries (mentor_role_changed→role + free_attempts_granted→certification, both actor=Cole). EXPLAIN ANALYZE confirmed planner picks `idx_super_admin_audit_log_affected_user_created` (Index Scan, 0.051ms execution, no seq scan, 3 buffer hits). Lovable's index concern resolved without new migration. **M4 `create_completion_bulk_rpcs`**: Three new SECDEF wrappers following `assign_curriculum_bulk` template. `set_content_item_completion_bulk(p_user_ids[], p_content_item_id, p_complete, p_reason)`, `set_module_completion_bulk(p_user_ids[], p_module_id, p_complete, p_reason)`, `set_curriculum_completion_bulk(p_user_ids[], p_curriculum_id, p_complete, p_reason)` — the curriculum variant resolves user→assignment_id internally, preferring active over completed, most recent assigned_at, per-user "no_curriculum_assignment_for_user" recorded as failure. Max 500 users per call. Each wrapper does BEGIN/EXCEPTION/END isolation per user, calls `assert_super_admin()` once at top, inherits impersonation gate from wrapped single-user RPCs (no double-gating). Returns standard `{operation, requested, succeeded, failed, results[]}` shape. Did NOT exercise as real bulk operations (would mark real content items complete); signature verification + structural match to `assign_curriculum_bulk` template sufficient at this phase. **M5 `add_completion_export_rpc`**: New SECDEF `get_user_completion_export(p_user_ids uuid[])` returning flat per-user-per-item rowset via UNION ALL across 4 tiers (cert_path from coach_certifications, curriculum from user_curriculum_assignments, module from user_module_assignments, content_item from content_item_completions). Columns: user_id, user_email, user_full_name, tier, target_id, target_name, parent_path (module breadcrumb for content_items via LEFT JOIN modules), status, started_at, completed_at, assigned_at. Max 500 users. Smoke test on Cole returned 2 cert_path rows (my_brainwise_coach certified + ptp_coach in_progress) + 1 curriculum row (PTP VILT 1 active) — expected shape. Frontend builds CSV from result. Final verification: 7-of-7 PASS check confirmed all deliverables present (M1 column, M2 14-arg signature, M3, M4a/b/c all three bulk RPCs, M5). (7) **Coach gate audit — 4 checks all clean.** Performed before M2 to ensure Coach tab plan holds. **Check 1**: `grant_additional_free_attempts` RPC body gates on `assert_super_admin + assert_impersonation_allows('permission_change')` only; does NOT require `account_type='coach'` on target. Cert row existence is sufficient. **Check 2**: `coach_certifications` RLS — three policies: service_role bypass + super_admin full access + `coaches read own (user_id = auth.uid())`. The "coaches read own" policy does NOT require `account_type='coach'`, so `is_practitioner_coach=true` users (including the 2 super_admins) can read their own cert rows. RLS is moot for drawer anyway since SECDEF bypasses RLS. **Check 3**: `pg_proc.prosrc ILIKE '%account_type%coach%'` returned 33 functions — most are content-fetching with coach-context permission checks, not gates affecting the Members Coach tab. Notable: `_sync_is_practitioner_coach_on_account_type` trigger auto-sets `is_practitioner_coach=true` when account_type becomes coach OR brainwise_super_admin — explains why all 10 coaches AND 2 super_admins have `is_practitioner_coach=true`. **Check 4**: `_sync_is_practitioner_coach_on_account_type` trigger body confirms the auto-sync. Coach tab visibility expression `is_practitioner_coach=true OR account_type='coach'` is equivalent to just `is_practitioner_coach=true` given the trigger — defensive OR doesn't hurt. **Conclusion**: plan holds without modification. Coach tab shows for `is_practitioner_coach=true OR account_type='coach'`; inside the tab, cert list shows for all; grant-attempts action enabled for all (RPC does not gate on account_type). Defer until Phase 11 ships and "Last login" tooltip semantics are operationally validated. (b) **`user_ui_preferences` dedicated table migration** — when 5+ admin surfaces have persisted prefs OR any query-into-preferences requirement emerges. Until then, jsonb-on-users column is fine. Migration is genuinely cheap when the day comes (one migration + one hook swap), so deferring is correct. (c) **Bulk role change** (deferred from Members v1 bulk-actions toolbar). (d) **Bulk MFA reset** (deferred from v1). (e) **Bulk password reset** (deferred from v1). (f) **Bulk send message** (deferred from v1; prerequisite is messaging subsystem). (10) **Standing rules to consider for v91 architecture-reference:** Four candidates emerged. **§121 candidate — Caller-owns-mutation pattern for shared action dialogs**: when a "shared" dialog would otherwise require a discriminated union of action types (each with different RPC, payload, invalidation, error mapping), invert ownership: dialog provides visual + UX + justification-field consistency, caller passes mutation function as prop. Avoids ugly internal switches and ages better. Trade-off: callers carry slightly more post-action cleanup responsibility, but the cleanup is genuinely caller-specific (different RPCs invalidate different keys). **§122 candidate — jsonb-on-row prefs vs table-of-prefs decision criterion**: for per-user preferences scoped to a single admin surface, column-on-users jsonb is fine. Migrate to dedicated table when 5+ surfaces have persisted prefs OR any query-into-preferences requirement emerges. Document write-from-frontend / read-whole-blob-on-mount contract in column comment to prevent accidental GIN-indexing or jsonb_path_query in WHERE clauses. Include `"version": 1` field for future schema evolution detection. **§123 candidate — Bulk RPC cap vs frontend chunking discipline**: bulk RPC cap matches existing pattern in the codebase for consistency (current: 500). Frontend chunking + progress UI ships independently as UX improvement, not as a backend timeout workaround. Chunks of 50-100 are pragmatic; cancel aborts the loop on frontend (each chunk RPC commits independently). Post-cancel UI must be honest: "Cancelled. {N} of {total} processed." not "Cancelled. Nothing was changed." **§124 candidate — Saved view detachment pattern (Linear style)**: when a UI surface has both saved views and inline filter controls, chip toggles detach the active view into an unsaved state rather than overwriting it. Indicator: leading `●` dot before view name (VS Code/Figma convention). Discard requires confirmation when 3+ changes detected. View-switch while detached uses three-button dialog [Cancel] [Discard] [Save and switch]. Cole picks the right subset for v91 in closeout; some may be too Phase 11-specific to warrant a §-number and become process notes instead. (11) **Session 87 close artifacts**: this v95 build-queue entry, architecture-reference v91 (selected from candidates §121-§124 above), session-87-to-88.md handoff, plus 4 design-phase docs (learning-admin-competitor-recon.md, phase-11-learners-surface-decisions.md, phase-11-lovable-review-prompt.md, phase-11-lovable-review-pass2.md) for upload to `cbastianBWE/brainwise-internal-docs` (flat repo root). Markdown only — Session 74 decision.
