### Build Queue items NEW Session 104 (continued) — G8a SHIPPED

**[SHIPPED] G8a — newsletter dispatch engine (backend + frontend), per-recipient tracking**

G8 split into G8a (dispatch engine, serving confirmed opt-in subscribers — no consent ambiguity) and G8b (in-product opt-in for logged-in users — the consent-laden part) and G8c (compliance hardening + automatic-mode wiring). G8a shipped this session.

Consent model decision LOCKED (Cole): users span US + EU + UK + Canada, so build for the strictest regime (GDPR + CASL) = explicit opt-in, demonstrable consent, no silent auto-subscribe. Becoming a paid user does NOT create newsletter consent. This collapses the "paid vs public subscriber" distinction: both are just people who explicitly opted in, one unified newsletter_subscribers list, one consent standard, one unsubscribe path. NOTE: Claude is not a lawyer; the architecture is the standard compliant pattern but a real compliance review is warranted before enabling at scale for EU/CA users.

Email format decision (Cole): summary (excerpt/seo_description) + opening of the article (first text-bearing TipTap blocks) + "Read full article" button to the site. Deliberately NOT full-content email (better deliverability, drives site traffic, avoids spam filters).

Backend shipped + verified:
- Migration `session104_g8a_dispatch_schema`: NEW `newsletter_settings` (singleton row, `dispatch_trigger_mode` 'manual'|'automatic' with CHECK, seeded 'manual'), NEW `newsletter_dispatches` (one row per send: article_id, triggered_by, trigger_type, status pending|sending|completed|failed|partial, recipient/sent/failed counts, timestamps), and ADDITIVE `email_logs` columns `dispatch_id` (FK→newsletter_dispatches), `opened_at`, `clicked_at`. All RLS = inline super-admin EXISTS + service_role_all, mirroring established pattern. Verified post-apply.
- NEW Edge Function `newsletter-dispatch` v1 (Class A, verify_jwt:true, super-admin gated, impersonation gate 'outbound_user_communication'). Takes {article_id, trigger_type}, validates article is published+not-archived (else 409), creates dispatch row, loads status='confirmed' subscribers (suppression by status — unsubscribed/bounced/complained/pending all excluded), per recipient: generates fresh raw unsubscribe token + stores its sha256 hash in newsletter_subscribers.unsubscribe_token_hash (Option 3 — reuses existing unsubscribe_from_newsletter(p_token) RPC unchanged), builds email-safe HTML (inline styles, table layout, opening text from first 4 TipTap paragraph/heading blocks, Read-full-article button, compliant footer w/ physical address 8735 Dunwoody Place #STE R Atlanta GA 30350 + working per-recipient unsubscribe link), sends via Resend direct POST (from: BrainWise Newsletter <newsletter@mail.brainwiseenterprises.com> — verified domain), logs each to email_logs (email_type='newsletter', dispatch_id, resend_message_id), updates dispatch counts+status. Auth perimeter verified (no-auth POST/GET → gateway 401, OPTIONS → 204).
- `resend-webhook` v4→v5: ADDITIVE 2-line change mapping email.opened→opened_at and email.clicked→clicked_at. All prior behavior (Svix verify, delivered/bounced/complained, subscriber status flips) byte-for-byte preserved. verify_jwt:false preserved (Svix signature is the auth gate).

Frontend shipped + verified (Lovable, planned-then-approved-then-built, verified against repo):
- NEW components under src/components/super-admin/newsletter/: SendDispatchButton (invokes newsletter-dispatch with correct body, gates on status==='published', handles 409, invalidates ["newsletter-dispatches", articleId]), DispatchHistoryPanel (lists newsletter_dispatches by article, newest first), DispatchEngagementStats (reads email_logs filtered by dispatch_id AND email_type='newsletter', counts delivered/opened/clicked/bounced from non-null timestamps), AutoSendToggle (reads/writes newsletter_settings.dispatch_trigger_mode directly, helper text states auto-send not yet wired).
- Edited AdminNewsletterArticle.tsx (Send button by StatusPill + dispatch history collapsible card in right aside) and AdminNewsletter.tsx (AutoSendToggle in page header). No backend changes from the Lovable cycle. Verified.

KEY PATTERN LEARNED — Edge Function _shared module path under this deploy tool: the documented `../_shared/...` import (from older functions) FAILS to bundle via the MCP deploy_edge_function tool ("Module not found"). The tool places the entrypoint at source/index.ts and co-locates bundled files under the SAME root, so a file named "_shared/impersonation_gate.ts" must be imported as `./_shared/...` NOT `../_shared/...`. Confirmed by deploy failure then success. Future Class A function deploys via MCP must use `./_shared/`.

**[OPEN — next] G8b (in-product opt-in) + G8c (compliance hardening + auto-send wiring)**

G8b: explicit opt-in surface for logged-in users (settings toggle and/or onboarding checkbox, unchecked by default) that writes a newsletter_subscribers row with linked_user_id set + consent_evidence recorded (in-product affirmative opt-in). Needs a backend opt-in RPC + a Lovable cycle. Reuses the existing unified list + unsubscribe.

G8c: wire publish_article → newsletter-dispatch when dispatch_trigger_mode='automatic' (guarded to fire only on genuine draft/scheduled→published transition, NOT on edits/re-saves of already-published articles); per-region consent-capture polish; enable email.opened + email.clicked events in the Resend DASHBOARD (Cole step — webhook already handles them, Resend must be told to emit them).

**[REMINDER] G8a smoke-test prerequisites:** zero confirmed subscribers currently, so a send reports 0 recipients + all-zero stat tiles (correct, not a bug). A real end-to-end send needs ≥1 confirmed subscriber (G8b creates these, or insert a confirmed test row). Open/click tiles stay 0 until the email.opened/email.clicked events are enabled in the Resend dashboard.

### Session 104 (continued) — G8b SHIPPED

**[SHIPPED] G8b — in-product newsletter opt-in (settings toggle + signup checkbox)**

Consent model: explicit affirmative opt-in only (GDPR/CASL/CAN-SPAM strictest-fits-all). Demonstrable consent recorded via consent_evidence='in_product_optin' + confirmed_at + linked_user_id. Logged-in user's account email is verified-by-ownership, so no email double-opt-in loop for in-product opt-in.

Backend shipped + verified — migration `session104_g8b_in_product_optin_rpcs`, three SECDEF RPCs, granted authenticated+service_role (NOT anon, §140 discipline):
- opt_in_to_newsletter(): upsert-by-email (email has UNIQUE constraint). No row → insert confirmed+linked+consent. unsubscribed → re-confirm+relink+re-record consent. confirmed/pending → idempotent ensure-linked-confirmed. bounced/complained → DO NOT auto-resurrect (Cole's call): link user for record only, return {success:false, error:'delivery_problem'}. Calls _sync_to_resend_audience_internal(id,'add') on success.
- opt_out_of_newsletter(): token-free (for settings toggle), finds by linked_user_id or email, sets unsubscribed, sync 'remove'. Idempotent.
- get_my_newsletter_subscription(): returns {subscribed:boolean, status}. Null-auth returns {subscribed:false,status:null} cleanly (verified).

Frontend shipped + verified (Lovable, planned→approved→built→verified against repo):
- NEW src/lib/newsletterOptInIntent.ts — localStorage intent flag WITH 24h TTL (consent-freshness: stamps Date.now() on set; consume removes key + returns true only if <24h old; try/catch fail-safe to false).
- src/pages/SignUp.tsx — separate UNCHECKED Checkbox (id=newsletter-opt-in), visually + logically distinct from terms checkbox. On submit, if checked, calls setPendingNewsletterOptIn() only — does NOT call opt_in inline (no session yet at signup-submit).
- src/hooks/useAuth.tsx — SIGNED_IN handler flushes pending intent: early-returns if none, calls opt_in_to_newsletter fire-and-forget in its own function, fully isolated from syncSubscription (a newsletter failure cannot affect sign-in). Fires once (flag consumed on read). Handles delivery_problem with support toast.
- src/pages/NotificationSettings.tsx — self-contained NewsletterSubscriptionCard: reads get_my_newsletter_subscription, optimistic Switch with revert() rollback, opt_in/opt_out on toggle, delivery_problem → revert + distinct support message. Separate Card (subscription, not a per-event channel pref).

Auth-timing handoff limitation (accepted, fail-safe): if user verifies on a different device than signup, the localStorage flag isn't present → no opt-in fires. Fails toward not-subscribing (compliant direction). Settings toggle is the fallback. Server-side intent storage deliberately NOT built.

NOTE: Claude is not a lawyer; architecture is the standard compliant pattern but real compliance review warranted before EU/CA scale.

### Resend dashboard state (Session 104, Cole-configured)
- Click tracking: ON (domain mail.brainwiseenterprises.com). Reliable engagement signal.
- Open tracking: OFF — Resend flags "Not Recommended" (pixel hurts deliverability + unreliable). Decision: leave OFF. opened_at column + Opened stat tile intentionally stay empty. webhook handles email.opened if ever enabled, but not subscribed.
- resend-webhook event subscriptions: was email.sent/delivered/bounced/complained/delivery_delayed (5). Cole ADDED email.clicked this session. email.opened intentionally NOT added.
- OPEN OPTIONAL (deliverability polish, needs DNS, not G8): custom tracking subdomain — Resend banner flags shared tracking domain. Defer.

### Session 104 (continued) — G8c backend SHIPPED (scheduled publish + auto-dispatch)

**[SHIPPED] G8c backend — scheduled-publish engine + automatic-mode dispatch wiring**

CRITICAL GAP FOUND + FIXED: the frontend could schedule an article (schedule_article RPC sets status='scheduled' + scheduled_for), but NOTHING published due scheduled articles — no process function, no cron. Scheduled articles would sit forever. Now fixed.

Design (Cole approved): Option A (full fix), conservative (no refactor of working authed publish_article/schedule_article — process_due contains its own transition logic mirroring publish_article), cron cadence every 15 min.

Stages all applied + verified:
- Stage 1 (migration session104_g8c_scheduled_by_user_id): ADD scheduled_by_user_id uuid to newsletter_articles (nullable FK→users) to attribute cron auto-publish snapshot + audit to the scheduling super-admin.
- Stage 2 (session104_g8c_schedule_article_capture_scheduler): schedule_article now sets scheduled_by_user_id=auth.uid(). ONLY change; rest byte-identical to deployed version.
- Stage 3 (session104_g8c_snapshot_scheduled_actor_fallback): _snapshot_article_version — when auth.uid() is null, fall back to current_setting('app.scheduled_article_actor'). When auth.uid() present (every existing caller) behavior byte-identical. Mirrors log_super_admin_action's existing scheduled-actor fallback pattern.
- Stage 4 (session104_g8c_process_due_scheduled_articles): NEW process_due_scheduled_articles() SECDEF, granted service_role only. Loops status='scheduled' AND archived_at IS NULL AND scheduled_for<=now(), per-article exception block (one bad article can't abort batch). Sets app.scheduled_article_actor + app.scheduled_assignment_actor to the article's scheduled_by_user_id so snapshot + audit attribute correctly. Mirrors publish_article transition (guards incl. gated-excerpt, UPDATE published, snapshot 'Published vN', audit log mode='scheduled_auto_publish'). Returns {processed, published_ids, dispatch_ids (only if mode=automatic), trigger_mode, failed[]}. VERIFIED end-to-end: scheduled a test draft, ran function, confirmed publish + 'Published v1' snapshot attributed to super-admin + audit row mode=scheduled_auto_publish; then restored test article to draft + deleted test snapshot. (One immutable audit row remains from the test — super_admin_audit_log blocks DELETE by design; harmless.)
- Stage 5 (newsletter-dispatch v1→v2): ADDITIVE dual-auth. A valid x-dispatcher-secret header (matching DISPATCHER_SHARED_SECRET env, same secret dispatch-grace-reminders uses) authenticates the service/cron path (skips JWT/super-admin/impersonation, triggered_by_user_id=null, trigger_type forced 'automatic'). Absent/invalid secret → original super-admin JWT path UNCHANGED. verify_jwt flipped true→false (gateway can't require JWT when secret path is allowed; in-function checks are the gate, matching dispatch-grace-reminders + resend-webhook pattern). Auth perimeter RE-VERIFIED: no-auth→401, bad secret→falls to JWT path→401, bad JWT→401 invalid_jwt, OPTIONS→204. safeEqual constant-time comparison.
- Stage 6 (session104_g8c_cron_publish_dispatch_wrapper): NEW cron_publish_and_dispatch_due_articles() SECDEF service_role only — calls process_due_scheduled_articles(), then for each dispatch_id does net.http_post to newsletter-dispatch with x-dispatcher-secret (vault departure_dispatcher_shared_secret), best-effort per article. Cron job 'publish_and_dispatch_due_articles' scheduled '*/15 * * * *', active. VERIFIED registered + dry-run clean.

KEY LESSON: newsletter_articles has CHECK newsletter_articles_scheduled_consistency = ((status='scheduled' AND scheduled_for IS NOT NULL AND scheduled_for > now()) OR status<>'scheduled'). Cannot directly force a past scheduled_for while status='scheduled' (test harness gotcha). Real path is fine: schedule sets future time; cron publish flips status away from 'scheduled' so the CHECK's second branch passes. CHECK only evaluated on write, not continuously, so a row whose scheduled_for has passed sits valid until the cron updates it.

**[OPEN — last G8 piece] G8c frontend: manual-publish auto-dispatch**
When a super-admin publishes manually via the UI AND newsletter_settings.dispatch_trigger_mode='automatic', the browser (already authenticated) should call newsletter-dispatch with trigger_type:'automatic' after a successful publish_article. This is the ONLY remaining G8 build. Scheduled publishes already auto-dispatch server-side (Stage 6). Lovable cycle, plan-first. (Manual publishes don't go through the cron, so they need this frontend trigger; without it, automatic mode only auto-sends scheduled publishes, not manual ones.)

### Session 104 (continued) — G8c frontend SHIPPED → G8 COMPLETE

**[SHIPPED] G8c frontend — manual-publish auto-dispatch**

Edit-only to src/pages/super-admin/AdminNewsletterArticle.tsx, inside runTransition. Verified against repo:
- prevStatus captured before the transition. Auto-dispatch gated on kind==='publish' AND (prevStatus==='draft' OR prevStatus==='scheduled'). Re-publish (prevStatus==='unpublished') is SUPPRESSED (Cole's call) — manual Send button remains the only re-blast path.
- When gate passes, direct select of newsletter_settings.dispatch_trigger_mode (manual-as-default on error/null); if 'automatic', invoke newsletter-dispatch with {article_id, trigger_type:'automatic'}.
- Decoupling guards all present: publish-failure early return before the block; dispatch in its own nested try/catch that only toasts + swallows; dialog cleanup (setTransitionDialog(null)/clear reason/setHydrated(false)/refreshArticle()) runs unconditionally after. A dispatch failure never makes a successful publish look failed.
- 409 handled distinctly; ["newsletter-dispatches", id] invalidated on success. Nothing outside runTransition touched.

**G8 COMPLETE** — all of G8a (dispatch engine + per-recipient tracking), G8b (in-product opt-in, settings toggle + signup checkbox), G8c (scheduled-publish engine + automatic-mode dispatch, server-side for scheduled + frontend for manual) shipped and verified, backend and frontend.

Coverage summary of automatic mode:
- Manual UI publish (draft/scheduled→published) in automatic mode → frontend fires dispatch (G8c frontend).
- Scheduled publish (cron) in automatic mode → server-side cron fires dispatch via secret path (G8c Stage 6).
- Re-publish (unpublished→published) → never auto-dispatches in either path; manual Send button only.
- Manual mode → nothing auto-sends; the Send to subscribers button is the only path.
